posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:The Legend Hotel, adjacent to the Xi'an Municipal Government, has a superior geographical location. The manor-style historical building is well-maintained both inside and outside, with a high green coverage rate. Several large ginkgo trees show its value. If you stay here in autumn, it will be a different scene. There is a small museum on the first floor of the hotel, which records the glorious history of the hotel and the heavyweight foreign guests it has received. Although I stayed here for only two nights during the May Day holiday, I could feel the courtesy and enthusiasm of the hotel waiters from the moment I got off the car at the hotel entrance. They carried my luggage, opened the door and showed me the way, greeted me when I met them, and responded to my requests. Special praise to the two Butlers Gu Yan and Yang Fan who received me and my husband. They upgraded my room type when the occupancy rate was very high during the holiday, and arranged a high-floor side suite. The room was clean and reasonably laid out, with a bathroom at each end, which met all my expectations for hotel accommodation. During the stay, Legend provided guests with a semi-buffet breakfast service on a la carte basis. Both Chinese and Western specialties were well prepared, and the appetite was well controlled, demonstrating the quality that a long-established five-star hotel should have. In the evening from 17:30 to 19:30, the lounge on the 7th floor also provides free happy hour for guests. There are not many dishes, but the quality is not ambiguous at all, and the types are changed every day. On the second day of check-in, the housekeeper Xiao Gu called me to confirm the specific time of cleaning the room. The housekeeper Xiao Yang was able to delay the check-out by one hour on the day of our departure as requested. Every little bit is full of sincerity. My husband and I plan to come to Xi'an to see the ginkgo again in autumn, and we will definitely choose the Legend Hotel next timeğŸ‘

Breakfast is a combination of buffet and a la carte. In addition to the buffet, there are two pages of menus to choose from. Basically, they have all the specialties of Xi'an. A suggestion: Basically, the service staff during the check-in period are very friendly and enthusiastic, but when we arrived and when we left, the luggage was brought in by ourselves. On the day of check-in, it is said that because the guests just arrived at the front, the service staff went to pick up the front luggage. On the day we left, we waited for the car in the lobby for a while before leaving. Maybe the service staff felt that they had already checked out and did not need to serve. As a result, our three suitcases came and went by the old people and children lifting up and down the stairs at the door to the car at the door. This has never happened before in other luxury hotels. This experience does not match the star rating of your hotel. I hope that the service at this price can last from beginning to end.

msg:Sofitel Legend Xi'an has a superior geographical location, rich historical content, and caring personnel, and its reputation is well-deserved.

When I checked in during the epidemic, the front desk staff was full of enthusiasm. I checked the very detailed nucleic acid testing locations and working hours to inform the guests, which was very convenient. Danny, the front office manager, led us to do an in-depth tour of the hotel. We visited the hotel museum, public areas and guest rooms of different grades. We learned about the various bonuses of the number 53. The hotel uses the original floor for cutting and resurfacing. It is very moving to feel his strong pride in such a building that bears witness to history.

But the hotel does have some flaws. The room was remodeled from the original room. The layout is strange and the area is too small. It has been a long time since I have seen a twin room with two 1-meter beds. In the end, the reason why I temporarily changed the check-in time and left the store early was the lack of catering during the epidemic. The original happy hour only had a few sweet and salty snacks, French fries and chicken nuggets. Like breakfast, I need to go to the Sofitel next door to pick them up. , is a complete downgrade. On the morning of the third day of check-in, my own restaurant opened, but the variety of food was limited, but not up to the existing standard. In fact, if you feel that there are too few guests to guarantee the catering package, you don't have to open it at all. Such a downgrade will fool you and you don't know what the hotel considers.

Finally, I would like to thank the staff for their hard work, and recommend it to everyone who pays attention to historical value and can tolerate some settings that do not meet modern hotel settings.
